msg:Conrad is located above the Meimei 1 shopping mall. Its tall and unique facade stands out among the buildings in the Youhao Road business district. Check-in is on the 37th floor. A square pool lined with tall chandeliers and translucent partition walls heighten the style of the lobby. The floor-to-ceiling glass can directly face the east side of the city and overlook the Tianshan Mountains. The front desk space is relatively small, and the seating area capacity is also very limited. When checking in, proactively provide information on attractions, visiting spots, and food around the hotel, which is thoughtful and considerate. The complimentary Hilton card holder is also an unexpected surprise.
The style room is located in the east part of the hotel floor, with an area of ‚Äã‚Äã60 square meters. The layout is like a studio, with hosts and guests, and they are all fully automatic toilets. The special floor plan of the hotel makes the bedroom plan form a right-angled trapezoid, and the shower space is not square. The black and white marble floor tiles are very prominent in the hotel's overall brown and yellow decoration color scheme, but the floor temperature is very low, so it is recommended not to walk barefoot. The floors in the bedroom and cloakroom are wooden floors, with floor heating, making them comfortable no matter how you walk. The cloakroom has a floor-to-ceiling mirror and ample space for drying clothes. The wall of the bedroom is decorated with Western-style patterns unique to Urumqi Conrad, and the asymmetric bed lamps (one lamp, one hanging) are all designed in ancient style, which is very elegant. There are a burgundy leather sofa and a Morandi green cloth sofa on both sides of the big bed, as well as three round tables. The minibar is hidden in the floor-to-ceiling cabinet in the corner, making the bedroom look neat and elegant. Floor-to-ceiling windows offer views of Urumqi‚Äôs classic business district, Hongshan Park and Yamalik Mountain in the distance.
Breakfast is at the CENTRO restaurant on the 6th floor. The dishes are quite rich, but the hot dishes are not as many as those at Hilton. The specialty is that there is an a la carte menu, and the eggs Benedict and steak are both delicious. Milk tea is a Kazakh flavor.
The swimming pool is located on the 7th floor. From the elevator to the entrance, you have to walk through a winding corridor and walk up a flight of steps. It is really like walking through the employee passage. Safety officer Xiao Yang helped pour hot water to relieve the discomfort caused by swimming dehydration and dry throat. The service was very good and I gave it a thumbs up. The space design is quite high-end, but there is no massage pool. The water temperature is on the low side, so you have to swim to get used to it. There are fewer people swimming in winter, so the feeling of private swimming is still very enjoyable.
